30   private val defaultMethodFilter = new NameFilter {
31     def apply(pre: Type, name: Name)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean = name.is(DefaultGetterName)
32   }
33 
34   /** Only one overloaded alternative is allowed to define default arguments */
35   private def checkOverloadedRestrictions(clazz: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit = {
36     // Using the default getters (such as methodName$default$1) as a cheap way of
37     // finding methods with default parameters. This way, we can limit the members to
38     // those with the DEFAULTPARAM flag, and infer the methods. Looking for the methods
39     // directly requires inspecting the parameter list of every one. That modification
40     // shaved 95% off the time spent in this method.
41 
42     for (
43       defaultGetterClass <- List(clazz, clazz.companionModule.moduleClass);
44       if defaultGetterClass.isClass
45     ) {
46       val defaultGetterNames = defaultGetterClass.asClass.memberNames(defaultMethodFilter)
47       val defaultMethodNames = defaultGetterNames map { _ rewrite {
48         case DefaultGetterName(methName, _) => methName
49       }}
50 
51       for (name <- defaultMethodNames) {
52         val methods = clazz.info.member(name).alternatives.map(_.symbol)
53         val haveDefaults = methods.filter(_.hasDefaultParams)
54         if (haveDefaults.length > 1) {
55           val owners = haveDefaults map (_.owner)
56           // constructors of different classes are allowed to have defaults
57           if (haveDefaults.exists(x => !x.isConstructor) || owners.distinct.size < haveDefaults.size)
58             ctx.error(
59               "in " + clazz +
60                 ", multiple overloaded alternatives of " + haveDefaults.head +
61                 " define default arguments" + (
62                   if (owners.forall(_ == clazz)) "."
63                   else ".\nThe members with defaults are defined in " + owners.map(_.showLocated).mkString("", " and ", ".")),
64               clazz.pos)
65         }
66       }
67     }
68 
69     // Check for doomed attempt to overload applyDynamic
70     if (clazz derivesFrom defn.DynamicClass) {
71       for ((_, m1 :: m2 :: _) <- (clazz.info member nme.applyDynamic).alternatives groupBy (_.symbol.typeParams.length)) {
72         ctx.error("implementation restriction: applyDynamic cannot be overloaded except by methods with different numbers of type parameters, e.g. applyDynamic[T1](method: String)(arg: T1) and applyDynamic[T1, T2](method: String)(arg1: T1, arg2: T2)",
73           m1.symbol.pos)
74       }
75     }
76   }
77 
78   /** The this-type of `cls` which should be used when looking at the types of
79    *  inherited members. If `cls` has a non-trivial self type, this returns a skolem
80    *  with the class type instead of the `this-type` of the class as usual.
81    *  This is done because otherwise we want to understand inherited infos
82    *  as they are written, whereas with the this-type they could be
83    *  more special. A test where this makes a difference is pos/i1401.scala.
84    *  This one used to succeed only if forwarding parameters is on.
85    *  (Forwarding tends to hide problems by binding parameter names).
86    */
87   private def upwardsThisType(cls: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context) = cls.info match {
88     case ClassInfo(_, _, _, _, tp: Type) if (tp ne cls.typeRef) && !cls.is(ModuleOrFinal) =>
89       SkolemType(cls.appliedRef).withName(nme.this_)
90     case _ =>
91       cls.thisType
92   }
93 
94   /** Check that self type of this class conforms to self types of parents.
95    *  and required classes.
96    */
97   private def checkParents(cls: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit = cls.info match {
98     case cinfo: ClassInfo =>
99       def checkSelfConforms(other: ClassSymbol, category: String, relation: String) = {
100         val otherSelf = other.givenSelfType.asSeenFrom(cls.thisType, other.classSymbol)
101         if (otherSelf.exists && !(cinfo.selfType <:< otherSelf))
102           ctx.error(DoesNotConformToSelfType(category, cinfo.selfType, cls, otherSelf, relation, other.classSymbol),
103             cls.pos)
104       }
105       for (parent <- cinfo.classParents)
106         checkSelfConforms(parent.typeSymbol.asClass, "illegal inheritance", "parent")
107       for (reqd <- cinfo.cls.givenSelfType.classSymbols)
108         checkSelfConforms(reqd, "missing requirement", "required")
109     case _ =>
110   }
111 
112   /** Check that a class and its companion object to not both define
113    *  a class or module with same name
114    */
115   private def checkCompanionNameClashes(cls: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit =
116     if (!cls.owner.is(ModuleClass)) {
117       def clashes(sym: Symbol) =
118         sym.isClass &&
119         sym.name.stripModuleClassSuffix == cls.name.stripModuleClassSuffix
120 
121       val others = cls.owner.linkedClass.info.decls.filter(clashes)
122       others.foreach { other =>
123         ctx.error(ClassAndCompanionNameClash(cls, other), cls.pos)
124       }
125     }

127   // Override checking ------------------------------------------------------------
128 
129   /** 1. Check all members of class `clazz` for overriding conditions.
130    *  That is for overriding member M and overridden member O:
131    *
132    *    1.1. M must have the same or stronger access privileges as O.
133    *    1.2. O must not be effectively final.
134    *    1.3. O is deferred, or M has `override` modifier.
135    *    1.4. If O is stable, then so is M.
136    *     // @M: LIFTED 1.5. Neither M nor O are a parameterized type alias
137    *    1.6. If O is a type alias, then M is an alias of O.
138    *    1.7. If O is an abstract type then
139    *       1.7.1 either M is an abstract type, and M's bounds are sharper than O's bounds.
140    *             or M is a type alias or class which conforms to O's bounds.
141    *       1.7.2 higher-order type arguments must respect bounds on higher-order type parameters  -- @M
142    *              (explicit bounds and those implied by variance annotations) -- @see checkKindBounds
143    *    1.8. If O and M are values, then
144    *    1.8.1  M's type is a subtype of O's type, or
145    *    1.8.2  M is of type []S, O is of type ()T and S <: T, or
146    *    1.8.3  M is of type ()S, O is of type []T and S <: T, or
147    *    1.9    M must not be a Dotty macro def
148    *    1.10.  If M is a 2.x macro def, O cannot be deferred unless there's a concrete method overriding O.
149    *    1.11.  If M is not a macro def, O cannot be a macro def.
150    *  2. Check that only abstract classes have deferred members
151    *  3. Check that concrete classes do not have deferred definitions
152    *     that are not implemented in a subclass.
153    *  4. Check that every member with an `override` modifier
154    *     overrides some other member.
155    *  TODO check that classes are not overridden
156    *  TODO This still needs to be cleaned up; the current version is a staright port of what was there
157    *       before, but it looks too complicated and method bodies are far too large.
158    */
159   private def checkAllOverrides(clazz: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit = {
160     val self = clazz.thisType
161     val upwardsSelf = upwardsThisType(clazz)
162     var hasErrors = false
163 
164     case class MixinOverrideError(member: Symbol, msg: String)
165 
166     val mixinOverrideErrors = new mutable.ListBuffer[MixinOverrideError]()
167 
168     def printMixinOverrideErrors(): Unit = {
169       mixinOverrideErrors.toList match {
170         case List() =>
171         case List(MixinOverrideError(_, msg)) =>
172           ctx.error(msg, clazz.pos)
173         case MixinOverrideError(member, msg) :: others =>
174           val others1 = others.map(_.member).filter(_.name != member.name).distinct
175           def othersMsg = {
176             val others1 = others.map(_.member)
177               .filter(_.name != member.name)
178               .map(_.show).distinct
179             if (others1.isEmpty) ""
180             else i";\nother members with override errors are:: $others1%, %"
181           }
182           ctx.error(msg + othersMsg, clazz.pos)
183       }
184     }
185 
186     def infoString(sym: Symbol) = infoString0(sym, sym.owner != clazz)
187     def infoStringWithLocation(sym: Symbol) = infoString0(sym, true)
188 
189     def infoString0(sym: Symbol, showLocation: Boolean) = {
190       val sym1 = sym.underlyingSymbol
191       def info = self.memberInfo(sym1)
192       val infoStr =
193         if (sym1.isAliasType) i", which equals ${info.bounds.hi}"
194         else if (sym1.isAbstractOrParamType) i" with bounds$info"
195         else if (sym1.is(Module)) ""
196         else if (sym1.isTerm) i" of type $info"
197         else ""
198       i"${if (showLocation) sym1.showLocated else sym1}$infoStr"
199     }
200 
201     /* Check that all conditions for overriding `other` by `member`
202        * of class `clazz` are met.
203        */
204     def checkOverride(member: Symbol, other: Symbol): Unit = {
205       def memberTp(self: Type) =
206         if (member.isClass) TypeAlias(member.typeRef.EtaExpand(member.typeParams))
207         else self.memberInfo(member)
208       def otherTp(self: Type) = self.memberInfo(other)
209 
210       ctx.debuglog("Checking validity of %s overriding %s".format(member.showLocated, other.showLocated))
211 
212       def noErrorType = !memberTp(self).isErroneous && !otherTp(self).isErroneous
213 
214       def overrideErrorMsg(msg: String): String = {
215         val isConcreteOverAbstract =
216           (other.owner isSubClass member.owner) && other.is(Deferred) && !member.is(Deferred)
217         val addendum =
218           if (isConcreteOverAbstract)
219             ";\n  (Note that %s is abstract,\n  and is therefore overridden by concrete %s)".format(
220               infoStringWithLocation(other),
221               infoStringWithLocation(member))
222           else if (ctx.settings.Ydebug.value)
223             err.typeMismatchMsg(memberTp(self), otherTp(self))
224           else ""
225 
226         "error overriding %s;\n  %s %s%s".format(
227           infoStringWithLocation(other), infoString(member), msg, addendum)
228       }
229 
230       def emitOverrideError(fullmsg: String) =
231         if (!(hasErrors && member.is(Synthetic) && member.is(Module))) {
232           // suppress errors relating toi synthetic companion objects if other override
233           // errors (e.g. relating to the companion class) have already been reported.
234           if (member.owner == clazz) ctx.error(fullmsg, member.pos)
235           else mixinOverrideErrors += new MixinOverrideError(member, fullmsg)
236           hasErrors = true
237         }
238 
239       def overrideError(msg: String) = {
240         if (noErrorType)
241           emitOverrideError(overrideErrorMsg(msg))
242       }
243 
244       def autoOverride(sym: Symbol) =
245         sym.is(Synthetic) && (
246           desugar.isDesugaredCaseClassMethodName(member.name) || // such names are added automatically, can't have an override preset.
247           sym.is(Module)) // synthetic companion
248 
249       def overrideAccessError() = {
250         ctx.log(i"member: ${member.showLocated} ${member.flags}") // DEBUG
251         ctx.log(i"other: ${other.showLocated} ${other.flags}") // DEBUG
252         val otherAccess = (other.flags & AccessFlags).toString
253         overrideError("has weaker access privileges; it should be " +
254           (if (otherAccess == "") "public" else "at least " + otherAccess))
255       }
256 
257       def compatibleTypes(memberTp: Type, otherTp: Type): Boolean =
258         try
259           if (member.isType) // intersection of bounds to refined types must be nonempty
260             memberTp.bounds.hi.hasSameKindAs(otherTp.bounds.hi) &&
261             ((memberTp frozen_<:< otherTp) ||
262              !member.owner.derivesFrom(other.owner) && {
263                // if member and other come from independent classes or traits, their
264                // bounds must have non-empty-intersection
265                val jointBounds = (memberTp.bounds & otherTp.bounds).bounds
266                jointBounds.lo frozen_<:< jointBounds.hi
267              })
268           else
269             member.name.is(DefaultGetterName) || // default getters are not checked for compatibility
270             memberTp.overrides(otherTp,
271                 member.matchNullaryLoosely || other.matchNullaryLoosely ||
272                 ctx.testScala2Mode(overrideErrorMsg("no longer has compatible type"),
273                    (if (member.owner == clazz) member else clazz).pos))
274         catch {
275           case ex: MissingType =>
276             // can happen when called with upwardsSelf as qualifier of memberTp and otherTp,
277             // because in that case we might access types that are not members of the qualifier.
278             false
279         }
280 
281       //Console.println(infoString(member) + " overrides " + infoString(other) + " in " + clazz);//DEBUG
282 
283       // return if we already checked this combination elsewhere
284       if (member.owner != clazz) {
285         def deferredCheck = member.is(Deferred) || !other.is(Deferred)
286         def subOther(s: Symbol) = s derivesFrom other.owner
287         def subMember(s: Symbol) = s derivesFrom member.owner
288 
289         if (subOther(member.owner) && deferredCheck) {
290           //Console.println(infoString(member) + " shadows1 " + infoString(other) " in " + clazz);//DEBUG
291           return
292         }
293         val parentSymbols = clazz.info.parents.map(_.typeSymbol)
294         if (parentSymbols exists (p => subOther(p) && subMember(p) && deferredCheck)) {
295           //Console.println(infoString(member) + " shadows2 " + infoString(other) + " in " + clazz);//DEBUG
296           return
297         }
298         if (parentSymbols forall (p => subOther(p) == subMember(p))) {
299           //Console.println(infoString(member) + " shadows " + infoString(other) + " in " + clazz);//DEBUG
300           return
301         }
302       }
303 
304       /* Is the intersection between given two lists of overridden symbols empty? */
305       def intersectionIsEmpty(syms1: Iterator[Symbol], syms2: Iterator[Symbol]) = {
306         val set2 = syms2.toSet
307         !(syms1 exists (set2 contains _))
308       }
309 
310       // o: public | protected        | package-protected  (aka java's default access)
311       // ^-may be overridden by member with access privileges-v
312       // m: public | public/protected | public/protected/package-protected-in-same-package-as-o
313 
314       if (member.is(Private)) // (1.1)
315         overrideError("has weaker access privileges; it should not be private")
316 
317       // todo: align accessibility implication checking with isAccessible in Contexts
318       val ob = other.accessBoundary(member.owner)
319       val mb = member.accessBoundary(member.owner)
320       def isOverrideAccessOK = (
321         (member.flags & AccessFlags).isEmpty // member is public
322         || // - or -
323         (!other.is(Protected) || member.is(Protected)) && // if o is protected, so is m, and
324         (ob.isContainedIn(mb) || other.is(JavaProtected)) // m relaxes o's access boundary,
325         // or o is Java defined and protected (see #3946)
326         )
327       if (!isOverrideAccessOK) {
328         overrideAccessError()
329       } else if (other.isClass) {
330         // direct overrides were already checked on completion (see Checking.chckWellFormed)
331         // the test here catches indirect overriddes between two inherited base types.
332         overrideError("cannot be used here - class definitions cannot be overridden")
333       } else if (!other.is(Deferred) && member.isClass) {
334         overrideError("cannot be used here - classes can only override abstract types")
335       } else if (other.isEffectivelyFinal) { // (1.2)
336         overrideError(i"cannot override final member ${other.showLocated}")
337       } else if (!other.is(Deferred) &&
338                  !other.name.is(DefaultGetterName) &&
339                  !member.isAnyOverride) {
340         // (*) Exclusion for default getters, fixes SI-5178. We cannot assign the Override flag to
341         // the default getter: one default getter might sometimes override, sometimes not. Example in comment on ticket.
342         // Also excluded under Scala2 mode are overrides of default methods of Java traits.
343         if (autoOverride(member) ||
344             other.owner.is(JavaTrait) && ctx.testScala2Mode("`override' modifier required when a Java 8 default method is re-implemented", member.pos))
345           member.setFlag(Override)
346         else if (member.owner != clazz && other.owner != clazz && !(other.owner derivesFrom member.owner))
347           emitOverrideError(
348             clazz + " inherits conflicting members:\n  "
349               + infoStringWithLocation(other) + "  and\n  " + infoStringWithLocation(member)
350               + "\n(Note: this can be resolved by declaring an override in " + clazz + ".)")
351         else
352           overrideError("needs `override' modifier")
353       } else if (other.is(AbsOverride) && other.isIncompleteIn(clazz) && !member.is(AbsOverride)) {
354         overrideError("needs `abstract override' modifiers")
355       } else if (member.is(Override) && other.is(Accessor) &&
356         other.accessedFieldOrGetter.is(Mutable, butNot = Lazy)) {
357         // !?! this is not covered by the spec. We need to resolve this either by changing the spec or removing the test here.
358         // !!! is there a !?! convention? I'm !!!ing this to make sure it turns up on my searches.
359         if (!ctx.settings.YoverrideVars.value)
360           overrideError("cannot override a mutable variable")
361       } else if (member.isAnyOverride &&
362         !(member.owner.thisType.baseClasses exists (_ isSubClass other.owner)) &&
363         !member.is(Deferred) && !other.is(Deferred) &&
364         intersectionIsEmpty(member.extendedOverriddenSymbols, other.extendedOverriddenSymbols)) {
365         overrideError("cannot override a concrete member without a third member that's overridden by both " +
366           "(this rule is designed to prevent ``accidental overrides'')")
367       } else if (other.isStable && !member.isStable) { // (1.4)
368         overrideError("needs to be a stable, immutable value")
369       } else if (member.is(ModuleVal) && !other.isRealMethod && !other.is(Deferred | Lazy)) {
370         overrideError("may not override a concrete non-lazy value")
371       } else if (member.is(Lazy, butNot = Module) && !other.isRealMethod && !other.is(Lazy) &&
372                  !ctx.testScala2Mode("may not override a non-lazy value", member.pos)) {
373         overrideError("may not override a non-lazy value")
374       } else if (other.is(Lazy) && !other.isRealMethod && !member.is(Lazy)) {
375         overrideError("must be declared lazy to override a lazy value")
376       } else if (member.is(Macro, butNot = Scala2x)) { // (1.9)
377         overrideError("is a macro, may not override anything")
378       } else if (other.is(Deferred) && member.is(Scala2Macro) && member.extendedOverriddenSymbols.forall(_.is(Deferred))) { // (1.10)
379         overrideError("cannot be used here - term macros cannot override abstract methods")
380       } else if (other.is(Macro) && !member.is(Macro)) { // (1.11)
381         overrideError("cannot be used here - only term macros can override term macros")
382       } else if (!compatibleTypes(memberTp(self), otherTp(self)) &&
383                  !compatibleTypes(memberTp(upwardsSelf), otherTp(upwardsSelf))) {
384         overrideError("has incompatible type" + err.whyNoMatchStr(memberTp(self), otherTp(self)))
385       } else {
386         checkOverrideDeprecated()
387       }
388     }
389 
390     /* TODO enable; right now the annotation is scala-private, so cannot be seen
391          * here.
392          */
393     def checkOverrideDeprecated() = { /*
394           if (other.hasDeprecatedOverridingAnnotation) {
395             val suffix = other.deprecatedOverridingMessage map (": " + _) getOrElse ""
396             val msg = s"overriding ${other.fullLocationString} is deprecated$suffix"
397             unit.deprecationWarning(member.pos, msg)
398           }*/
399     }
400 
401     try {
402       val opc = new OverridingPairs.Cursor(clazz)
403       while (opc.hasNext) {
404         checkOverride(opc.overriding, opc.overridden)
405         opc.next()
406       }
407     } catch {
408       case ex: MergeError =>
409         val addendum = ex.tp1 match {
410           case tp1: ClassInfo =>
411             "\n(Note that having same-named member classes in types of a mixin composition is no longer allowed)"
412           case _ => ""
413         }
414         ctx.error(ex.getMessage + addendum, clazz.pos)
415     }
416     printMixinOverrideErrors()
417 
418     // Verifying a concrete class has nothing unimplemented.
419     if (!clazz.is(AbstractOrTrait)) {
420       val abstractErrors = new mutable.ListBuffer[String]
421       def abstractErrorMessage =
422         // a little formatting polish
423         if (abstractErrors.size <= 2) abstractErrors mkString " "
424         else abstractErrors.tail.mkString(abstractErrors.head + ":\n", "\n", "")
425 
426       def abstractClassError(mustBeMixin: Boolean, msg: String): Unit = {
427         def prelude = (
428           if (clazz.isAnonymousClass || clazz.is(Module)) "object creation impossible"
429           else if (mustBeMixin) clazz + " needs to be a mixin"
430           else clazz + " needs to be abstract") + ", since"
431 
432         if (abstractErrors.isEmpty) abstractErrors ++= List(prelude, msg)
433         else abstractErrors += msg
434       }
435 
436       def hasJavaErasedOverriding(sym: Symbol): Boolean =
437         !ctx.erasurePhase.exists || // can't do the test, assume the best
438           ctx.atPhase(ctx.erasurePhase.next) { implicit ctx =>
439             clazz.info.nonPrivateMember(sym.name).hasAltWith { alt =>
440               alt.symbol.is(JavaDefined, butNot = Deferred) &&
441                 !sym.owner.derivesFrom(alt.symbol.owner) &&
442                 alt.matches(sym)
443             }
444           }
445 
446       def ignoreDeferred(member: SingleDenotation) =
447         member.isType ||
448           member.symbol.isSuperAccessor || // not yet synthesized
449           member.symbol.is(JavaDefined) && hasJavaErasedOverriding(member.symbol)
450 
451       // 2. Check that only abstract classes have deferred members
452       def checkNoAbstractMembers(): Unit = {
453         // Avoid spurious duplicates: first gather any missing members.
454         val missing = clazz.thisType.abstractTermMembers.filterNot(ignoreDeferred)
455         // Group missing members by the name of the underlying symbol,
456         // to consolidate getters and setters.
457         val grouped: Map[Name, Seq[SingleDenotation]] = missing groupBy (_.symbol.underlyingSymbol.name)
458           // Dotty deviation: Added type annotation for `grouped`.
459           // The inferred type is Map[Symbol#ThisName, Seq[SingleDenotation]]
460           // but then the definition of isMultiple fails with an error:
461           // RefChecks.scala:379: error: type mismatch:
462           // found   : underlying.ThisName
463           // required: dotty.tools.dotc.core.Symbols.Symbol#ThisName
464           //
465           //  val isMultiple = grouped.getOrElse(underlying.name(ctx), Nil).size > 1
466           //                                                    ^
467           // As far as I can see, the complaint is correct, even under the
468           // old reading where Symbol#ThisName means x.ThisName forSome { val x }
469 
470         val missingMethods = grouped.toList flatMap {
471           case (name, syms) =>
472             val withoutSetters = syms filterNot (_.symbol.isSetter)
473             if (withoutSetters.nonEmpty) withoutSetters else syms
474         }
475 
476         def stubImplementations: List[String] = {
477           // Grouping missing methods by the declaring class
478           val regrouped = missingMethods.groupBy(_.symbol.owner).toList
479           def membersStrings(members: List[SingleDenotation]) =
480             members.sortBy(_.symbol.name.toString).map(_.showDcl + " = ???")
481 
482           if (regrouped.tail.isEmpty)
483             membersStrings(regrouped.head._2)
484           else (regrouped.sortBy("" + _._1.name) flatMap {
485             case (owner, members) =>
486               ("// Members declared in " + owner.fullName) +: membersStrings(members) :+ ""
487           }).init
488         }
489 
490         // If there are numerous missing methods, we presume they are aware of it and
491         // give them a nicely formatted set of method signatures for implementing.
492         if (missingMethods.size > 1) {
493           abstractClassError(false, "it has " + missingMethods.size + " unimplemented members.")
494           val preface =
495             """|/** As seen from %s, the missing signatures are as follows.
496                  | *  For convenience, these are usable as stub implementations.
497                  | */
498                  |""".stripMargin.format(clazz)
499           abstractErrors += stubImplementations.map("  " + _ + "\n").mkString(preface, "", "")
500           return
501         }
502 
503         for (member <- missing) {
504           val memberSym = member.symbol
505           def undefined(msg: String) =
506             abstractClassError(false, s"${member.showDcl} is not defined $msg")
507           val underlying = memberSym.underlyingSymbol
508 
509           // Give a specific error message for abstract vars based on why it fails:
510           // It could be unimplemented, have only one accessor, or be uninitialized.
511           if (underlying.is(Mutable)) {
512             val isMultiple = grouped.getOrElse(underlying.name(ctx), Nil).size > 1
513 
514             // If both getter and setter are missing, squelch the setter error.
515             if (memberSym.isSetter && isMultiple) ()
516             else undefined(
517               if (memberSym.isSetter) "\n(Note that an abstract var requires a setter in addition to the getter)"
518               else if (memberSym.isGetter && !isMultiple) "\n(Note that an abstract var requires a getter in addition to the setter)"
519               else err.abstractVarMessage(memberSym))
520           } else if (underlying.is(Method)) {
521             // If there is a concrete method whose name matches the unimplemented
522             // abstract method, and a cursory examination of the difference reveals
523             // something obvious to us, let's make it more obvious to them.
524             val abstractParams = underlying.info.firstParamTypes
525             val matchingName = clazz.info.nonPrivateMember(underlying.name).alternatives
526             val matchingArity = matchingName filter { m =>
527               !m.symbol.is(Deferred) &&
528                 m.info.firstParamTypes.length == abstractParams.length
529             }
530 
531             matchingArity match {
532               // So far so good: only one candidate method
533               case concrete :: Nil =>
534                 val mismatches =
535                   abstractParams.zip(concrete.info.firstParamTypes)
536                     .filterNot { case (x, y) => x =:= y }
537                 mismatches match {
538                   // Only one mismatched parameter: say something useful.
539                   case (pa, pc) :: Nil =>
540                     val abstractSym = pa.typeSymbol
541                     val concreteSym = pc.typeSymbol
542                     def subclassMsg(c1: Symbol, c2: Symbol) =
543                       s": ${c1.showLocated} is a subclass of ${c2.showLocated}, but method parameter types must match exactly."
544                     val addendum =
545                       if (abstractSym == concreteSym)
546                         (pa.typeConstructor, pc.typeConstructor) match {
547                           case (TypeRef(pre1, _), TypeRef(pre2, _)) =>
548                             if (pre1 =:= pre2) ": their type parameters differ"
549                             else ": their prefixes (i.e. enclosing instances) differ"
550                           case _ =>
551                             ""
552                         }
553                       else if (abstractSym isSubClass concreteSym)
554                         subclassMsg(abstractSym, concreteSym)
555                       else if (concreteSym isSubClass abstractSym)
556                         subclassMsg(concreteSym, abstractSym)
557                       else ""
558 
559                     undefined(s"\n(Note that ${pa.show} does not match ${pc.show}$addendum)")
560                   case xs =>
561                     undefined(s"\n(The class implements a member with a different type: ${concrete.showDcl})")
562                 }
563               case Nil =>
564                 undefined("")
565               case concretes =>
566                 undefined(s"\n(The class implements members with different types: ${concretes.map(_.showDcl)}%\n  %)")
567             }
568           } else undefined("")
569         }
570       }
571 
572       // 3. Check that concrete classes do not have deferred definitions
573       // that are not implemented in a subclass.
574       // Note that this is not the same as (2); In a situation like
575       //
576       // class C { def m: Int = 0}
577       // class D extends C { def m: Int }
578       //
579       // (3) is violated but not (2).
580       def checkNoAbstractDecls(bc: Symbol): Unit = {
581         for (decl <- bc.info.decls) {
582           if (decl.is(Deferred) && !ignoreDeferred(decl)) {
583             val impl = decl.matchingMember(clazz.thisType)
584             if (impl == NoSymbol || (decl.owner isSubClass impl.owner)) {
585               val impl1 = clazz.thisType.nonPrivateMember(decl.name) // DEBUG
586               ctx.log(i"${impl1}: ${impl1.info}") // DEBUG
587               ctx.log(i"${clazz.thisType.memberInfo(decl)}") // DEBUG
588               abstractClassError(false, "there is a deferred declaration of " + infoString(decl) +
589                 " which is not implemented in a subclass" + err.abstractVarMessage(decl))
590             }
591           }
592         }
593         if (bc.asClass.superClass.is(Abstract))
594           checkNoAbstractDecls(bc.asClass.superClass)
595       }
596 
597       checkNoAbstractMembers()
598       if (abstractErrors.isEmpty)
599         checkNoAbstractDecls(clazz)
600 
601       if (abstractErrors.nonEmpty)
602         ctx.error(abstractErrorMessage, clazz.pos)
603     } else if (clazz.is(Trait) && !(clazz derivesFrom defn.AnyValClass)) {
604       // For non-AnyVal classes, prevent abstract methods in interfaces that override
605       // final members in Object; see #4431
606       for (decl <- clazz.info.decls) {
607         // Have to use matchingSymbol, not a method involving overridden symbols,
608         // because the scala type system understands that an abstract method here does not
609         // override a concrete method in Object. The jvm, however, does not.
610         val overridden = decl.matchingDecl(defn.ObjectClass, defn.ObjectType)
611         if (overridden.is(Final))
612           ctx.error(TraitRedefinedFinalMethodFromAnyRef(overridden), decl.pos)
613       }
614     }
615 
616     /* Returns whether there is a symbol declared in class `inclazz`
617        * (which must be different from `clazz`) whose name and type
618        * seen as a member of `class.thisType` matches `member`'s.
619        */
620     def hasMatchingSym(inclazz: Symbol, member: Symbol): Boolean = {
621 
622       def isSignatureMatch(sym: Symbol) = !sym.isTerm ||
623         clazz.thisType.memberInfo(sym).matchesLoosely(member.info)
624 
625       /* The rules for accessing members which have an access boundary are more
626          * restrictive in java than scala.  Since java has no concept of package nesting,
627          * a member with "default" (package-level) access can only be accessed by members
628          * in the exact same package.  Example:
629          *
630          *   package a.b;
631          *   public class JavaClass { void foo() { } }
632          *
633          * The member foo() can be accessed only from members of package a.b, and not
634          * nested packages like a.b.c.  In the analogous scala class:
635          *
636          *   package a.b
637          *   class ScalaClass { private[b] def foo() = () }
638          *
639          * The member IS accessible to classes in package a.b.c.  The javaAccessCheck logic
640          * is restricting the set of matching signatures according to the above semantics.
641          */
642       def javaAccessCheck(sym: Symbol) = (
643         !inclazz.is(JavaDefined) // not a java defined member
644         || !sym.privateWithin.exists // no access boundary
645         || sym.is(Protected) // marked protected in java, thus accessible to subclasses
646         || sym.privateWithin == member.enclosingPackageClass // exact package match
647         )
648       def classDecls = inclazz.info.nonPrivateDecl(member.name)
649 
650       (inclazz != clazz) &&
651         classDecls.hasAltWith(d => isSignatureMatch(d.symbol) && javaAccessCheck(d.symbol))
652     }
653 
654     // 4. Check that every defined member with an `override` modifier overrides some other member.
655     for (member <- clazz.info.decls)
656       if (member.isAnyOverride && !(clazz.thisType.baseClasses exists (hasMatchingSym(_, member)))) {
657         if (checks != noPrinter) {
658           for (bc <- clazz.info.baseClasses.tail) {
659             val sym = bc.info.decl(member.name).symbol
660             if (sym.exists)
661               checks.println(i"$bc has $sym: ${clazz.thisType.memberInfo(sym)}")
662           }
663         }
664 
665         val nonMatching = clazz.info.member(member.name).altsWith(alt => alt.owner != clazz)
666         nonMatching match {
667           case Nil =>
668             ctx.error(OverridesNothing(member), member.pos)
669           case ms =>
670             ctx.error(OverridesNothingButNameExists(member, ms), member.pos)
671         }
672         member.resetFlag(Override)
673         member.resetFlag(AbsOverride)
674       }
675   }
676 
677   // Note: if a symbol has both @deprecated and @migration annotations and both
678   // warnings are enabled, only the first one checked here will be emitted.
679   // I assume that's a consequence of some code trying to avoid noise by suppressing
680   // warnings after the first, but I think it'd be better if we didn't have to
681   // arbitrarily choose one as more important than the other.
682   private def checkUndesiredProperties(sym: Symbol, pos: Position)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit = {
683     // If symbol is deprecated, and the point of reference is not enclosed
684     // in either a deprecated member or a scala bridge method, issue a warning.
685     if (sym.isDeprecated && !ctx.owner.ownersIterator.exists(_.isDeprecated)) {
686       ctx.deprecationWarning("%s is deprecated%s".format(
687         sym.showLocated, sym.deprecationMessage map (": " + _) getOrElse ""), pos)
688     }
689     // Similar to deprecation: check if the symbol is marked with @migration
690     // indicating it has changed semantics between versions.
691     val xMigrationValue = ctx.settings.Xmigration.value
692     if (sym.hasAnnotation(defn.MigrationAnnot) && xMigrationValue != NoScalaVersion) {
693       sym.migrationVersion.get match {
694         case scala.util.Success(symVersion) if xMigrationValue < symVersion=>
695           ctx.warning(SymbolChangedSemanticsInVersion(sym, symVersion), pos)
696         case Failure(ex) =>
697           ctx.warning(SymbolHasUnparsableVersionNumber(sym, ex.getMessage()), pos)
698         case _ =>
699       }
700     }
701     /*  (Not enabled yet)
702        *  See an explanation of compileTimeOnly in its scaladoc at scala.annotation.compileTimeOnly.
703        *
704       if (sym.isCompileTimeOnly) {
705         def defaultMsg =
706           sm"""Reference to ${sym.fullLocationString} should not have survived past type checking,
707               |it should have been processed and eliminated during expansion of an enclosing macro."""
708         // The getOrElse part should never happen, it's just here as a backstop.
709         ctx.error(sym.compileTimeOnlyMessage getOrElse defaultMsg, pos)
710       }*/
711   }
712 
713   /** Check that a deprecated val or def does not override a
714    *  concrete, non-deprecated method.  If it does, then
715    *  deprecation is meaningless.
716    */
717   private def checkDeprecatedOvers(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit = {
718     val symbol = tree.symbol
719     if (symbol.isDeprecated) {
720       val concrOvers =
721         symbol.allOverriddenSymbols.filter(sym =>
722           !sym.isDeprecated && !sym.is(Deferred))
723       if (!concrOvers.isEmpty)
724         ctx.deprecationWarning(
725           symbol.toString + " overrides concrete, non-deprecated symbol(s):" +
726             concrOvers.map(_.name).mkString("    ", ", ", ""), tree.pos)
727     }
728   }
729 
730   type LevelAndIndex = immutable.Map[Symbol, (LevelInfo, Int)]
731 
732   class OptLevelInfo extends DotClass {
733     def levelAndIndex: LevelAndIndex = Map()
734     def enterReference(sym: Symbol, pos: Position): Unit = ()
735   }
736 
737   /** A class to help in forward reference checking */
738   class LevelInfo(outerLevelAndIndex: LevelAndIndex, stats: List[Tree])(implicit ctx: Context)
739   extends OptLevelInfo {
740     override val levelAndIndex: LevelAndIndex =
741       ((outerLevelAndIndex, 0) /: stats) {(mi, stat) =>
742         val (m, idx) = mi
743         val m1 = stat match {
744           case stat: MemberDef => m.updated(stat.symbol, (this, idx))
745           case _ => m
746         }
747         (m1, idx + 1)
748       }._1
749     var maxIndex: Int = Int.MinValue
750     var refPos: Position = _
751     var refSym: Symbol = _
752 
753     override def enterReference(sym: Symbol, pos: Position): Unit =
754       if (sym.exists && sym.owner.isTerm)
755         levelAndIndex.get(sym) match {
756           case Some((level, idx)) if (level.maxIndex < idx) =>
757             level.maxIndex = idx
758             level.refPos = pos
759             level.refSym = sym
760           case _ =>
761         }
762   }
763 
764   val NoLevelInfo = new OptLevelInfo()
765 }
766 import RefChecks._
767 
768 /** Post-attribution checking and transformation, which fulfills the following roles
769  *
770  *  1. This phase performs the following checks.
771  *
772  *  - only one overloaded alternative defines default arguments
773  *  - applyDynamic methods are not overloaded
774  *  - all overrides conform to rules laid down by `checkAllOverrides`.
775  *  - any value classes conform to rules laid down by `checkDerivedValueClass`.
776  *  - this(...) constructor calls do not forward reference other definitions in their block (not even lazy vals).
777  *  - no forward reference in a local block jumps over a non-lazy val definition.
778  *  - a class and its companion object do not both define a class or module with the same name.
779  *
780  *  2. It warns about references to symbols labeled deprecated or migration.
781 
782  *  3. It eliminates macro definitions.
783  *
784  *  4. It makes members not private where necessary. The following members
785  *  cannot be private in the Java model:
786  *   - term members of traits
787  *   - the primary constructor of a value class
788  *   - the parameter accessor of a value class
789  *   - members accessed from an inner or companion class.
790  *  All these members are marked as NotJavaPrivate.
791  *  Unlike in Scala 2.x not-private members keep their name. It is
792  *  up to the backend to find a unique expanded name for them. The
793  *  rationale to do name changes that late is that they are very fragile.
794 
795  *  todo: But RefChecks is not done yet. It's still a somewhat dirty port from the Scala 2 version.
796  *  todo: move untrivial logic to their own mini-phases
797  */
798 class RefChecks extends MiniPhase { thisPhase =>
799 
800   import tpd._
801   import reporting.diagnostic.messages.ForwardReferenceExtendsOverDefinition
802   import dotty.tools.dotc.reporting.diagnostic.messages.UnboundPlaceholderParameter
803 
804   override def phaseName: String = "refchecks"
805 
806   // Needs to run after ElimRepeated for override checks involving varargs methods
807   override def runsAfter = Set(classOf[ElimRepeated])
808 
809   private var LevelInfo: Store.Location[OptLevelInfo] = _
810   private def currentLevel(implicit ctx: Context): OptLevelInfo = ctx.store(LevelInfo)
811 
812   override def initContext(ctx: FreshContext) =
813     LevelInfo = ctx.addLocation(NoLevelInfo)
814 
815   override def prepareForStats(trees: List[Tree])(implicit ctx: Context) =
816     if (ctx.owner.isTerm)
817       ctx.fresh.updateStore(LevelInfo, new LevelInfo(currentLevel.levelAndIndex, trees))
818     else ctx
819 
820   override def transformValDef(tree: ValDef)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
821     checkDeprecatedOvers(tree)
822     val sym = tree.symbol
823     if (sym.exists && sym.owner.isTerm) {
824       tree.rhs match {
825         case Ident(nme.WILDCARD) => ctx.error(UnboundPlaceholderParameter(), sym.pos)
826         case _ =>
827       }
828       if (!sym.is(Lazy)) {
829         currentLevel.levelAndIndex.get(sym) match {
830           case Some((level, symIdx)) if symIdx <= level.maxIndex =>
831             ctx.error(ForwardReferenceExtendsOverDefinition(sym, level.refSym), level.refPos)
832           case _ =>
833         }
834       }
835     }
836     tree
837   }
838 
839   override def transformDefDef(tree: DefDef)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
840     checkDeprecatedOvers(tree)
841     if (tree.symbol is Macro) EmptyTree else tree
842   }
843 
844   override def transformTemplate(tree: Template)(implicit ctx: Context) = try {
845     val cls = ctx.owner
846     checkOverloadedRestrictions(cls)
847     checkParents(cls)
848     checkCompanionNameClashes(cls)
849     checkAllOverrides(cls)
850     tree
851   } catch {
852     case ex: MergeError =>
853       ctx.error(ex.getMessage, tree.pos)
854       tree
855   }
856 
857   override def transformIdent(tree: Ident)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
858     checkUndesiredProperties(tree.symbol, tree.pos)
859     currentLevel.enterReference(tree.symbol, tree.pos)
860     tree
861   }
862 
863   override def transformSelect(tree: Select)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
864     checkUndesiredProperties(tree.symbol, tree.pos)
865     tree
866   }
867 
868   override def transformApply(tree: Apply)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
869     if (isSelfConstrCall(tree)) {
870       assert(currentLevel.isInstanceOf[LevelInfo], ctx.owner + "/" + i"$tree")
871       val level = currentLevel.asInstanceOf[LevelInfo]
872       if (level.maxIndex > 0) {
873         // An implementation restriction to avoid VerifyErrors and lazyvals mishaps; see SI-4717
874         ctx.debuglog("refsym = " + level.refSym)
875         ctx.error("forward reference not allowed from self constructor invocation", level.refPos)
876       }
877     }
878     tree
879   }
880 
881   override def transformNew(tree: New)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
882     val sym = tree.tpe.typeSymbol
883     checkUndesiredProperties(sym, tree.pos)
884     currentLevel.enterReference(sym, tree.pos)
885     tree
886   }
887 }
888 
889 /* todo: rewrite and re-enable
890 
891 // Comparison checking -------------------------------------------------------
892 
893     object normalizeAll extends TypeMap {
894       def apply(tp: Type) = mapOver(tp).normalize
895     }
896 
897     def checkImplicitViewOptionApply(pos: Position, fn: Tree, args: List[Tree]): Unit = if (settings.lint) (fn, args) match {
898       case (tap@TypeApply(fun, targs), List(view: ApplyImplicitView)) if fun.symbol == currentRun.runDefinitions.Option_apply =>
899         unit.warning(pos, s"Suspicious application of an implicit view (${view.fun}) in the argument to Option.apply.") // SI-6567
900       case _ =>
901     }
902 
903     private def isObjectOrAnyComparisonMethod(sym: Symbol) = sym match {
904       case Object_eq | Object_ne | Object_== | Object_!= | Any_== | Any_!= => true
905       case _                                                               => false
906     }
907     /** Check the sensibility of using the given `equals` to compare `qual` and `other`. */
908     private def checkSensibleEquals(pos: Position, qual: Tree, name: Name, sym: Symbol, other: Tree) = {
909       def isReferenceOp = sym == Object_eq || sym == Object_ne
910       def isNew(tree: Tree) = tree match {
911         case Function(_, _) | Apply(Select(New(_), nme.CONSTRUCTOR), _) => true
912         case _ => false
913       }
914       def underlyingClass(tp: Type): Symbol = {
915         val sym = tp.widen.typeSymbol
916         if (sym.isAbstractOrParamType) underlyingClass(sym.info.bounds.hi)
917         else sym
918       }
919       val actual   = underlyingClass(other.tpe)
920       val receiver = underlyingClass(qual.tpe)
921       def onTrees[T](f: List[Tree] => T) = f(List(qual, other))
922       def onSyms[T](f: List[Symbol] => T) = f(List(receiver, actual))
923 
924       // @MAT normalize for consistency in error message, otherwise only part is normalized due to use of `typeSymbol`
925       def typesString = normalizeAll(qual.tpe.widen)+" and " + normalizeAll(other.tpe.widen)
926 
927       /* Symbols which limit the warnings we can issue since they may be value types */
928       val isMaybeValue = Set[Symbol](AnyClass, AnyRefClass, AnyValClass, ObjectClass, ComparableClass, JavaSerializableClass)
929 
930       // Whether def equals(other: Any) has known behavior: it is the default
931       // inherited from java.lang.Object, or it is a synthetically generated
932       // case equals.  TODO - more cases are warnable if the target is a synthetic
933       // equals.
934       def isUsingWarnableEquals = {
935         val m = receiver.info.member(nme.equals_)
936         ((m == Object_equals) || (m == Any_equals) || isMethodCaseEquals(m))
937       }
938       def isMethodCaseEquals(m: Symbol) = m.isSynthetic && m.owner.isCase
939       def isCaseEquals = isMethodCaseEquals(receiver.info.member(nme.equals_))
940       // Whether this == or != is one of those defined in Any/AnyRef or an overload from elsewhere.
941       def isUsingDefaultScalaOp = sym == Object_== || sym == Object_!= || sym == Any_== || sym == Any_!=
942       def haveSubclassRelationship = (actual isSubClass receiver) || (receiver isSubClass actual)
943 
944       // Whether the operands+operator represent a warnable combo (assuming anyrefs)
945       // Looking for comparisons performed with ==/!= in combination with either an
946       // equals method inherited from Object or a case class synthetic equals (for
947       // which we know the logic.)
948       def isWarnable           = isReferenceOp || (isUsingDefaultScalaOp && isUsingWarnableEquals)
949       def isEitherNullable     = (NullTpe <:< receiver.info) || (NullTpe <:< actual.info)
950       def isEitherValueClass   = actual.isDerivedValueClass || receiver.isDerivedValueClass
951       def isBoolean(s: Symbol) = unboxedValueClass(s) == BooleanClass
952       def isUnit(s: Symbol)    = unboxedValueClass(s) == UnitClass
953       def isNumeric(s: Symbol) = isNumericValueClass(unboxedValueClass(s)) || isAnyNumber(s)
954       def isScalaNumber(s: Symbol) = s isSubClass ScalaNumberClass
955       def isJavaNumber(s: Symbol)  = s isSubClass JavaNumberClass
956       // includes java.lang.Number if appropriate [SI-5779]
957       def isAnyNumber(s: Symbol)     = isScalaNumber(s) || isJavaNumber(s)
958       def isMaybeAnyValue(s: Symbol) = isPrimitiveValueClass(unboxedValueClass(s)) || isMaybeValue(s)
959       // used to short-circuit unrelatedTypes check if both sides are special
960       def isSpecial(s: Symbol) = isMaybeAnyValue(s) || isAnyNumber(s)
961       val nullCount            = onSyms(_ filter (_ == NullClass) size)
962       def isNonsenseValueClassCompare = (
963            !haveSubclassRelationship
964         && isUsingDefaultScalaOp
965         && isEitherValueClass
966         && !isCaseEquals
967       )
968 
969       // Have we already determined that the comparison is non-sensible? I mean, non-sensical?
970       var isNonSensible = false
971 
972       def nonSensibleWarning(what: String, alwaysEqual: Boolean) = {
973         val msg = alwaysEqual == (name == nme.EQ || name == nme.eq)
974         unit.warning(pos, s"comparing $what using `${name.decode}' will always yield $msg")
975         isNonSensible = true
976       }
977       def nonSensible(pre: String, alwaysEqual: Boolean) =
978         nonSensibleWarning(s"${pre}values of types $typesString", alwaysEqual)
979       def nonSensiblyEq() = nonSensible("", alwaysEqual = true)
980       def nonSensiblyNeq() = nonSensible("", alwaysEqual = false)
981       def nonSensiblyNew() = nonSensibleWarning("a fresh object", alwaysEqual = false)
982 
983       def unrelatedMsg = name match {
984         case nme.EQ | nme.eq => "never compare equal"
985         case _               => "always compare unequal"
986       }
987       def unrelatedTypes() = if (!isNonSensible) {
988         val weaselWord = if (isEitherValueClass) "" else " most likely"
989         unit.warning(pos, s"$typesString are unrelated: they will$weaselWord $unrelatedMsg")
990       }
991 
992       if (nullCount == 2) // null == null
993         nonSensiblyEq()
994       else if (nullCount == 1) {
995         if (onSyms(_ exists isPrimitiveValueClass)) // null == 5
996           nonSensiblyNeq()
997         else if (onTrees( _ exists isNew)) // null == new AnyRef
998           nonSensiblyNew()
999       }
1000       else if (isBoolean(receiver)) {
1001         if (!isBoolean(actual) && !isMaybeValue(actual))    // true == 5
1002           nonSensiblyNeq()
1003       }
1004       else if (isUnit(receiver)) {
1005         if (isUnit(actual)) // () == ()
1006           nonSensiblyEq()
1007         else if (!isUnit(actual) && !isMaybeValue(actual))  // () == "abc"
1008           nonSensiblyNeq()
1009       }
1010       else if (isNumeric(receiver)) {
1011         if (!isNumeric(actual))
1012           if (isUnit(actual) || isBoolean(actual) || !isMaybeValue(actual))   // 5 == "abc"
1013             nonSensiblyNeq()
1014       }
1015       else if (isWarnable && !isCaseEquals) {
1016         if (isNew(qual)) // new X == y
1017           nonSensiblyNew()
1018         else if (isNew(other) && (receiver.isEffectivelyFinal || isReferenceOp))   // object X ; X == new Y
1019           nonSensiblyNew()
1020         else if (receiver.isEffectivelyFinal && !(receiver isSubClass actual) && !actual.isRefinementClass) {  // object X, Y; X == Y
1021           if (isEitherNullable)
1022             nonSensible("non-null ", false)
1023           else
1024             nonSensiblyNeq()
1025         }
1026       }
1027 
1028       // warn if one but not the other is a derived value class
1029       // this is especially important to enable transitioning from
1030       // regular to value classes without silent failures.
1031       if (isNonsenseValueClassCompare)
1032         unrelatedTypes()
1033       // possibleNumericCount is insufficient or this will warn on e.g. Boolean == j.l.Boolean
1034       else if (isWarnable && nullCount == 0 && !(isSpecial(receiver) && isSpecial(actual))) {
1035         // better to have lubbed and lost
1036         def warnIfLubless(): Unit = {
1037           val common = global.lub(List(actual.tpe, receiver.tpe))
1038           if (ObjectTpe <:< common)
1039             unrelatedTypes()
1040         }
1041         // warn if actual has a case parent that is not same as receiver's;
1042         // if actual is not a case, then warn if no common supertype, as below
1043         if (isCaseEquals) {
1044           def thisCase = receiver.info.member(nme.equals_).owner
1045           actual.info.baseClasses.find(_.isCase) match {
1046             case Some(p) if p != thisCase => nonSensible("case class ", false)
1047             case None =>
1048               // stronger message on (Some(1) == None)
1049               //if (receiver.isCase && receiver.isEffectivelyFinal && !(receiver isSubClass actual)) nonSensiblyNeq()
1050               //else
1051               // if a class, it must be super to thisCase (and receiver) since not <: thisCase
1052               if (!actual.isTrait && !(receiver isSubClass actual)) nonSensiblyNeq()
1053               else if (!haveSubclassRelationship) warnIfLubless()
1054             case _ =>
1055           }
1056         }
1057         // warn only if they have no common supertype below Object
1058         else if (!haveSubclassRelationship) {
1059           warnIfLubless()
1060         }
1061       }

1079   def overridesTypeInPrefix(tp1: Type, tp2: Type, prefix: Type): Boolean = (tp1.dealiasWiden, tp2.dealiasWiden) match {
1080     case (MethodType(List(), rtp1), NullaryMethodType(rtp2)) =>
1081       rtp1 <:< rtp2
1082     case (NullaryMethodType(rtp1), MethodType(List(), rtp2)) =>
1083       rtp1 <:< rtp2
1084     case (TypeRef(_, sym, _),  _) if sym.isModuleClass =>
1085       overridesTypeInPrefix(NullaryMethodType(tp1), tp2, prefix)
1086     case _ =>
1087       def classBoundAsSeen(tp: Type) = tp.typeSymbol.classBound.asSeenFrom(prefix, tp.typeSymbol.owner)
1088 
1089       (tp1 <:< tp2) || (  // object override check
1090         tp1.typeSymbol.isModuleClass && tp2.typeSymbol.isModuleClass && {
1091           val cb1 = classBoundAsSeen(tp1)
1092           val cb2 = classBoundAsSeen(tp2)
1093           (cb1 <:< cb2) && {
1094             log("Allowing %s to override %s because %s <:< %s".format(tp1, tp2, cb1, cb2))
1095             true
1096           }
1097         }
1098       )
1099   }
1100     private def checkTypeRef(tp: Type, tree: Tree, skipBounds: Boolean)(implicit ctx: Context) = tp match {
1101       case TypeRef(pre, sym, args) =>
1102         tree match {
1103           case tt: TypeTree if tt.original == null => // SI-7783 don't warn about inferred types
1104                                                       // FIXME: reconcile this check with one in resetAttrs
1105           case _ => checkUndesiredProperties(sym, tree.pos)
1106         }
1107         if (sym.isJavaDefined)
1108           sym.typeParams foreach (_.cookJavaRawInfo())
1109         if (!tp.isHigherKinded && !skipBounds)
1110           checkBounds(tree, pre, sym.owner, sym.typeParams, args)
1111       case _ =>
1112     }

1114     private def checkTypeRefBounds(tp: Type, tree: Tree) = {
1115       var skipBounds = false

1117         case AnnotatedType(ann :: Nil, underlying) if ann.symbol == UncheckedBoundsClass =>
1118           skipBounds = true
1119           underlying
1120         case TypeRef(pre, sym, args) =>
1121           if (!tp.isHigherKinded && !skipBounds)
1122             checkBounds(tree, pre, sym.owner, sym.typeParams, args)
1123           tp
1124         case _ =>
1125           tp
1126       }

1133     private def doTypeTraversal(tree: Tree)(f: Type => Unit) = if (!inPattern) tree.tpe foreach f

1135     private def applyRefchecksToAnnotations(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit = {
1136       def applyChecks(annots: List[Annotation]) = {
1137         checkAnnotations(annots map (_.atp), tree)
1138         transformTrees(annots flatMap (_.args))
1139       }

1142         case m: MemberDef =>

1145           // validate implicitNotFoundMessage

1147             unit.warning(tree.pos, f"Invalid implicitNotFound message for ${sym}%s${sym.locationString}%s:%n$warn")
1148           }

1150         case tpt@TypeTree() =>
1151           if (tpt.original != null) {
1152             tpt.original foreach {
1153               case dc@TypeTreeWithDeferredRefCheck() =>
1154                 applyRefchecksToAnnotations(dc.check()) // #2416
1155               case _ =>
1156             }
1157           }
1158 
1159           doTypeTraversal(tree) {
1160             case tp @ AnnotatedType(annots, _)  =>
1161               applyChecks(annots)
1162             case tp =>
1163           }
1164         case _ =>
1165       }

1168     private def transformCaseApply(tree: Tree, ifNot: => Unit) = {
1169       val sym = tree.symbol
1170 
1171       def isClassTypeAccessible(tree: Tree): Boolean = tree match {
1172         case TypeApply(fun, targs) =>
1173           isClassTypeAccessible(fun)
1174         case Select(module, apply) =>
1175           ( // SI-4859 `CaseClass1().InnerCaseClass2()` must not be rewritten to `new InnerCaseClass2()`;
1176             //          {expr; Outer}.Inner() must not be rewritten to `new Outer.Inner()`.
1177             treeInfo.isQualifierSafeToElide(module) &&
1178             // SI-5626 Classes in refinement types cannot be constructed with `new`. In this case,
1179             // the companion class is actually not a ClassSymbol, but a reference to an abstract type.
1180             module.symbol.companionClass.isClass
1181           )
1182       }
1183 
1184       val doTransform =
1185         sym.isRealMethod &&
1186         sym.isCase &&
1187         sym.name == nme.apply &&
1188         isClassTypeAccessible(tree)
1189 
1190       if (doTransform) {
1191         tree foreach {
1192           case i@Ident(_) =>
1193             enterReference(i.pos, i.symbol) // SI-5390 need to `enterReference` for `a` in `a.B()`
1194           case _ =>
1195         }
1196         toConstructor(tree.pos, tree.tpe)
1197       }
1198       else {
1199         ifNot
1200         tree
1201       }
1202     }

1204     private def transformApply(tree: Apply): Tree = tree match {
1205       case Apply(
1206         Select(qual, nme.filter | nme.withFilter),
1207         List(Function(
1208           List(ValDef(_, pname, tpt, _)),
1209           Match(_, CaseDef(pat1, _, _) :: _))))
1210         if ((pname startsWith nme.CHECK_IF_REFUTABLE_STRING) &&
1211             isIrrefutable(pat1, tpt.tpe) && (qual.tpe <:< tree.tpe)) =>
1212 
1213           transform(qual)
1214 
1215       case Apply(fn, args) =>
1216         // sensicality should be subsumed by the unreachability/exhaustivity/irrefutability
1217         // analyses in the pattern matcher
1218         if (!inPattern) {
1219           checkImplicitViewOptionApply(tree.pos, fn, args)
1220           checkSensible(tree.pos, fn, args)
1221         }
1222         currentApplication = tree
1223         tree
1224     }
1225     private def transformSelect(tree: Select): Tree = {
1226       val Select(qual, _) = tree
1227       val sym = tree.symbol
1228 
1229       checkUndesiredProperties(sym, tree.pos)
1230       checkDelayedInitSelect(qual, sym, tree.pos)
1231 
1232       if (!sym.exists)
1233         devWarning("Select node has NoSymbol! " + tree + " / " + tree.tpe)
1234       else if (sym.isLocalToThis)
1235         varianceValidator.checkForEscape(sym, currentClass)
1236 
1237       def checkSuper(mix: Name) =
1238         // term should have been eliminated by super accessors
1239         assert(!(qual.symbol.isTrait && sym.isTerm && mix == tpnme.EMPTY), (qual.symbol, sym, mix))
1240 
1241       transformCaseApply(tree,
1242         qual match {
1243           case Super(_, mix)  => checkSuper(mix)
1244           case _              =>
1245         }
1246       )
1247     }
1248     private def transformIf(tree: If): Tree = {
1249       val If(cond, thenpart, elsepart) = tree
1250       def unitIfEmpty(t: Tree): Tree =
1251         if (t == EmptyTree) Literal(Constant(())).setPos(tree.pos).setType(UnitTpe) else t
1252 
1253       cond.tpe match {
1254         case ConstantType(value) =>
1255           val res = if (value.booleanValue) thenpart else elsepart
1256           unitIfEmpty(res)
1257         case _ => tree
1258       }
1259     }

1261     // Warning about nullary methods returning Unit. TODO: move to lint
1262     private def checkNullaryMethodReturnType(sym: Symbol) = sym.tpe match {
1263       case NullaryMethodType(restpe) if restpe.typeSymbol == UnitClass =>
1264         // this may be the implementation of e.g. a generic method being parameterized
1265         // on Unit, in which case we had better let it slide.
1266         val isOk = (
1267              sym.isGetter
1268           || (sym.name containsName nme.DEFAULT_GETTER_STRING)
1269           || sym.allOverriddenSymbols.exists(over => !(over.tpe.resultType =:= sym.tpe.resultType))
1270         )
1271         if (!isOk)
1272           unit.warning(sym.pos, s"side-effecting nullary methods are discouraged: suggest defining as `def ${sym.name.decode}()` instead")
1273       case _ => ()
1274     }

1276     /* Convert a reference to a case factory of type `tpe` to a new of the class it produces. */
1277     def toConstructor(pos: Position, tpe: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
1278       val rtpe = tpe.finalResultType
1279       assert(rtpe.typeSymbol.is(Case), tpe)
1280       New(rtpe).withPos(pos).select(rtpe.typeSymbol.primaryConstructor)
1281     }
1282     private def isIrrefutable(pat: Tree, seltpe: Type): Boolean = pat match {
1283       case Apply(_, args) =>
1284         val clazz = pat.tpe.typeSymbol
1285         clazz == seltpe.typeSymbol &&
1286         clazz.isCaseClass &&
1287         (args corresponds clazz.primaryConstructor.tpe.asSeenFrom(seltpe, clazz).paramTypes)(isIrrefutable)
1288       case Typed(pat, tpt) =>
1289         seltpe <:< tpt.tpe
1290       case Ident(tpnme.WILDCARD) =>
1291         true
1292       case Bind(_, pat) =>
1293         isIrrefutable(pat, seltpe)
1294       case _ =>
1295         false
1296     }
1297     private def checkDelayedInitSelect(qual: Tree, sym: Symbol, pos: Position) = {
1298       def isLikelyUninitialized = (
1299            (sym.owner isSubClass DelayedInitClass)
1300         && !qual.tpe.isInstanceOf[ThisType]
1301         && sym.accessedOrSelf.isVal
1302       )
1303       if (settings.lint.value && isLikelyUninitialized)
1304         unit.warning(pos, s"Selecting ${sym} from ${sym.owner}, which extends scala.DelayedInit, is likely to yield an uninitialized value")
1305     }
1306     private def lessAccessible(otherSym: Symbol, memberSym: Symbol): Boolean = (
1307          (otherSym != NoSymbol)
1308       && !otherSym.isProtected
1309       && !otherSym.isTypeParameterOrSkolem
1310       && !otherSym.isExistentiallyBound
1311       && (otherSym isLessAccessibleThan memberSym)
1312       && (otherSym isLessAccessibleThan memberSym.enclClass)
1313     )
1314     private def lessAccessibleSymsInType(other: Type, memberSym: Symbol): List[Symbol] = {
1315       val extras = other match {
1316         case TypeRef(pre, _, args) =>
1317           // checking the prefix here gives us spurious errors on e.g. a private[process]
1318           // object which contains a type alias, which normalizes to a visible type.
1319           args filterNot (_ eq NoPrefix) flatMap (tp => lessAccessibleSymsInType(tp, memberSym))
1320         case _ =>
1321           Nil
1322       }
1323       if (lessAccessible(other.typeSymbol, memberSym)) other.typeSymbol :: extras
1324       else extras
1325     }
1326     private def warnLessAccessible(otherSym: Symbol, memberSym: Symbol) {
1327       val comparison = accessFlagsToString(memberSym) match {
1328         case ""   => ""
1329         case acc  => " is " + acc + " but"
1330       }
1331       val cannot =
1332         if (memberSym.isDeferred) "may be unable to provide a concrete implementation of"
1333         else "may be unable to override"
1334 
1335       unit.warning(memberSym.pos,
1336         "%s%s references %s %s.".format(
1337           memberSym.fullLocationString, comparison,
1338           accessFlagsToString(otherSym), otherSym
1339         ) + "\nClasses which cannot access %s %s %s.".format(
1340           otherSym.decodedName, cannot, memberSym.decodedName)
1341       )
1342     }

1344     /** Warn about situations where a method signature will include a type which
1345      *  has more restrictive access than the method itself.
1346      */
1347     private def checkAccessibilityOfReferencedTypes(tree: Tree) {
1348       val member = tree.symbol
1349 
1350       def checkAccessibilityOfType(tpe: Type) {
1351         val inaccessible = lessAccessibleSymsInType(tpe, member)
1352         // if the unnormalized type is accessible, that's good enough
1353         if (inaccessible.isEmpty) ()
1354         // or if the normalized type is, that's good too
1355         else if ((tpe ne tpe.normalize) && lessAccessibleSymsInType(tpe.dealiasWiden, member).isEmpty) ()
1356         // otherwise warn about the inaccessible syms in the unnormalized type
1357         else inaccessible foreach (sym => warnLessAccessible(sym, member))
1358       }
1359 
1360       // types of the value parameters
1361       mapParamss(member)(p => checkAccessibilityOfType(p.tpe))
1362       // upper bounds of type parameters
1363       member.typeParams.map(_.info.bounds.hi.widen) foreach checkAccessibilityOfType
1364     }

1375     override def transform(tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
1376       //val savedLocalTyper = localTyper
1377       try {
1378         val sym = tree.symbol
1379         checkOverloadedRestrictions(ctx.owner)
1380             checkAllOverrides(ctx.owner)
1381             checkAnyValSubclass(ctx.owner)
1382             if (ctx.owner.isDerivedValueClass)
1383               ctx.owner.primaryConstructor.makeNotPrivateAfter(NoSymbol, thisPhase) // SI-6601, must be done *after* pickler!
1384             tree
1385 
1386 
1387         // Apply RefChecks to annotations. Makes sure the annotations conform to
1388         // type bounds (bug #935), issues deprecation warnings for symbols used
1389         // inside annotations.
1390         // applyRefchecksToAnnotations(tree) ???
1391         var result: Tree = tree match {
1392           case tree: ValOrDefDef =>
1393             // move to lint:
1394             // if (settings.warnNullaryUnit)
1395             //  checkNullaryMethodReturnType(sym)
1396             // if (settings.warnInaccessible) {
1397             //  if (!sym.isConstructor && !sym.isEffectivelyFinal && !sym.isSynthetic)
1398             //    checkAccessibilityOfReferencedTypes(tree)
1399             // }
1400             // tree match {
1401             //  case dd: DefDef => checkByNameRightAssociativeDef(dd)
1402             //  case _          =>
1403             // }
1404             tree
1405 
1406           case Template(constr, parents, self, body) =>
1407             // localTyper = localTyper.atOwner(tree, currentOwner)
1408             checkOverloadedRestrictions(ctx.owner)
1409             checkAllOverrides(ctx.owner)
1410             checkAnyValSubclass(ctx.owner)
1411             if (ctx.owner.isDerivedValueClass)
1412               ctx.owner.primaryConstructor.makeNotPrivateAfter(NoSymbol, thisPhase) // SI-6601, must be done *after* pickler!
1413             tree
1414 
1415           case tpt: TypeTree =>
1416             transform(tpt.original)
1417             tree
1418 
1419           case TypeApply(fn, args) =>
1420             checkBounds(tree, NoPrefix, NoSymbol, fn.tpe.typeParams, args map (_.tpe))
1421             transformCaseApply(tree, ())
1422 
1423           case x @ Apply(_, _)  =>
1424             transformApply(x)
1425 
1426           case x @ If(_, _, _)  =>
1427             transformIf(x)
1428 
1429           case New(tpt) =>
1430             enterReference(tree.pos, tpt.tpe.typeSymbol)
1431             tree
1432 
1433           case treeInfo.WildcardStarArg(_) if !isRepeatedParamArg(tree) =>
1434             unit.error(tree.pos, "no `: _*' annotation allowed here\n" +
1435               "(such annotations are only allowed in arguments to *-parameters)")
1436             tree
1437 
1438           case Ident(name) =>
1439             checkUndesiredProperties(sym, tree.pos)
1440             transformCaseApply(tree,
1441               if (name != nme.WILDCARD && name != tpnme.WILDCARD_STAR) {
1442                 assert(sym != NoSymbol, "transformCaseApply: name = " + name.debugString + " tree = " + tree + " / " + tree.getClass) //debug
1443                 enterReference(tree.pos, sym)
1444               }
1445             )
1446 
1447           case x @ Select(_, _) =>
1448             transformSelect(x)
1449 
1450           case UnApply(fun, args) =>
1451             transform(fun) // just make sure we enterReference for unapply symbols, note that super.transform(tree) would not transform(fun)
1452                            // transformTrees(args) // TODO: is this necessary? could there be forward references in the args??
1453                            // probably not, until we allow parameterised extractors
1454             tree
1455 
1456 
1457           case _ => tree
1458         }
1459 
1460         // skip refchecks in patterns....
1461         result = result match {
1462           case CaseDef(pat, guard, body) =>
1463             val pat1 = savingInPattern {
1464               inPattern = true
1465               transform(pat)
1466             }
1467             treeCopy.CaseDef(tree, pat1, transform(guard), transform(body))
1468           case LabelDef(_, _, _) if treeInfo.hasSynthCaseSymbol(result) =>
1469             savingInPattern {
1470               inPattern = true
1471               deriveLabelDef(result)(transform)
1472             }
1473           case Apply(fun, args) if fun.symbol.isLabel && treeInfo.isSynthCaseSymbol(fun.symbol) =>
1474             savingInPattern {
1475               // SI-7756 If we were in a translated pattern, we can now switch out of pattern mode, as the label apply signals
1476               //         that we are in the user-supplied code in the case body.
1477               //
1478               //         Relies on the translation of:
1479               //            (null: Any) match { case x: List[_] => x; x.reverse; case _ => }'
1480               //         to:
1481               //            <synthetic> val x2: List[_] = (x1.asInstanceOf[List[_]]: List[_]);
1482               //                  matchEnd4({ x2; x2.reverse}) // case body is an argument to a label apply.
1483               inPattern = false
1484               super.transform(result)
1485             }
1486           case ValDef(_, _, _, _) if treeInfo.hasSynthCaseSymbol(result) =>
1487             deriveValDef(result)(transform) // SI-7716 Don't refcheck the tpt of the synthetic val that holds the selector.
1488           case _ =>
1489             super.transform(result)
1490         }
1491         result match {
1492           case ClassDef(_, _, _, _)
1493              | TypeDef(_, _, _, _) =>
1494             if (result.symbol.isLocalToBlock || result.symbol.isTopLevel)
1495               varianceValidator.traverse(result)
1496           case tt @ TypeTree() if tt.original != null =>
1497             varianceValidator.traverse(tt.original) // See SI-7872
1498           case _ =>
1499         }
1500 
1501         checkUnexpandedMacro(result)
1502 
1503         result
1504       } catch {
1505         case ex: TypeError =>
1506           if (settings.debug) ex.printStackTrace()
1507           unit.error(tree.pos, ex.getMessage())
1508           tree
1509       } finally {
1510         localTyper = savedLocalTyper
1511         currentApplication = savedCurrentApplication
1512       }
1513     }
